\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SendRequest()}{SendRequest()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::future$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{a01984}{Cpp\+PTSLResponse}} $>$ Send\+Request (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{a01980}{Cpp\+PTSLRequest}}}]{request,  }\item[{std\+::function$<$ void(const \mbox{\hyperlink{a01984}{Cpp\+PTSLResponse}} \&)$>$}]{response\+Callback = {\ttfamily nullptr} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sends a JSON-\/based request to Pro Tools. 

response\+Callback provides an ability to process all respones (both intermediate and final) in realtime. The callback is called from the service thread.

Get task execution status

Only returns the status of the task that is currently in progress. So it should be called asynchronously in parallel to the requested PTSL Command like it is implemented in PTSLC\+\_\+\+CPP\+::\+Cpp\+PTSLClient\+::\+Ping\+Task\+Status.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
task execution status 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{a01328_a2fb834727f02bdc4db8432508b5a8ed6}\label{a01328_a2fb834727f02bdc4db8432508b5a8ed6}} 
\index{CppPTSLClient@{CppPTSLClient}!ExportMix@{ExportMix}}
\index{ExportMix@{ExportMix}!CppPTSLClient@{CppPTSLClient}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ExportMix()}{ExportMix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{a01376}{Command\+Response}} $>$ Export\+Mix (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{a01560}{Export\+Mix\+Request}} \&}]{request }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}



Render all or part of the session to one or more files. 

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{a00467__deprecated000042}{Deprecated}}]All the API-\/specific functions (commands) are deprecated starting in Pro Tools 2024.\+10. Please use a general JSON-\/based \mbox{\hyperlink{a01328_a2c6a9bfa639cab78fcb3d4159c460c5f}{Send\+Request}} function instead.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Export Mix (Bounce Mix) can export an entire mix, including sub-\/mixes, to multiple file formats without having to create extra dedicated audio tracks in the session for bus recording. Different options and settings are available depending on the selected File\+Type. The options are organized in sections including Audio, Video, Location, and Dolby Atmos. Here\textquotesingle{}s a breakdown of how the sections are used for each File\+Type\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item WAV
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item has no Video section
\item has a unique field called Delivery\+Format (only shown if Interleaved is selected as the file format and there are multiple mix sources)
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item AIF
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item has no Video section
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item MP3
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item has no Video section
\item does not allow multiple mix sources
\item does not allow mix sources greater than 0
\item does not allow specifying Bit Depth value (always a 16Bit)
\item Sample Rate is limited to 48k and 44.\+1k
\item Import after Bounce is not available
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item MXF OPAtom
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item has no Video section
\item File format is multi-\/mono
\item Bit Depth is only 16Bit and 24Bit
\item Sample Rate is limited to 48k and 44.\+1k
\item Pad to frame boundary is hard-\/coded to ON
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item WAV (Dolby Atmos ADM BWF)
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item has no Audio section
\item has no Video section
\item has Dolby Atmos section (unique to this format)
\item has FFOA (bool) default to False
\item if FFOA is true then there\textquotesingle{}s an option to enter Time\+Code value
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Time\+Code value will match the session frame rate
\item Frame rate will always be 23.\+976 and 30 non-\/drop (if Frame rate is 60 -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} it will still be 30)
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item has Embed Program-\/level Metadata
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Task execution status 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyItemize}

Get dynamic properties from the host application

Use dynamic properties to query the application about its support for features such as codecs that are not directly bound to a particular version of the API or host application.

Removes memory locations corresponding to the numbers provided in the list. Memory location enumeration should start with 1 (using 0 or negative numbers may result in undefined behavior).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
task execution status and count of successfully and unsuccessfully cleared memory locations 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{a01888}{Get\+Session\+IDs\+Response}} $>$ Get\+Session\+IDs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{a01372}{Command\+Request}} \&}]{request }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [virtual]}}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{a00467__deprecated000105}{Deprecated}}]All the API-\/specific functions (commands) are deprecated starting in Pro Tools 2024.\+10. Please use a general JSON-\/based \mbox{\hyperlink{a01328_a2c6a9bfa639cab78fcb3d4159c460c5f}{Send\+Request}} function instead.\end{DoxyRefDesc}


Returns origin\+Id, instance\+Id and parent\+Id of the current opened session\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item origin\+Id is the main ID of the session (or project), and it remains the same in all variations of the session through Save As, Save Copy In, etc.
\item instance\+Id is unique for each session variation. In a new/original session file, the instance\+Id is equal to origin\+Id. When variants are introduced via Save As, Save Copy In, and several others, instance\+Id is set to a new unique ID.
\item parent\+Id is set to the instance\+Id of the source session for sessions based off of a previous session. For new/original sessions, the parent\+Id is set to zeros. That means parent\+Id is equal to origin\+Id for first-\/generation variants, and is different for second and later generation variations. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

References \mbox{\hyperlink{a01328_a13902e2669d5eb3b3f4deec3b50afb63}{Cpp\+PTSLClient\+::\+Get\+Session\+IDs()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{a00023_a970444c7bb1f588f120415d7764e509d}{INIT\+\_\+\+HNDLR}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{a00023_a18785599017f06817b6c0fb4eb115ca1}{MAKE\+\_\+\+REQUEST}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{a00023_ac61506f99035fc3573e9c8761268da0b}{MAKE\+\_\+\+RESP\+\_\+\+OVRD}}.



Referenced by \mbox{\hyperlink{a01328_a13902e2669d5eb3b3f4deec3b50afb63}{Cpp\+PTSLClient\+::\+Get\+Session\+IDs()}}.
